     * close elastic press autosuggest field

    $(document).on("click",".ep-autosuggest",function(e) {
            if (e.clientX > $(this).offset().left + $(this).width() &&
                e.clientY < $(this).offset().top + 30) {
                $(this).hide();
            }
        });

    $(document).on("click","body",function(e){
        if(!document.querySelector('.ep-autosuggest').contains(e.target)){
            $(".ep-autosuggest").hide();
        }
